                                    7718              Ÿ  THIS ROUTINE SCANS AND SKIPS AN EXPRESSION, AN ERROR WILL          Ÿ
                                    7719              Ÿ  BE RETURNED IF THE EXPRESSION IS INVALID.  (EG. DIVIDE BY          Ÿ
                                    7720              Ÿ  BY ZERO. UNDECLARED VARIABLE. ETC. ETC.)  THIS ROUTINE IS          Ÿ

                                    7722              Ÿ  EXPRESSION SCANNER IS A LOT OF WORK, SO WE JUST EVALUATE IT.       Ÿ

                                    7732              Ÿ       R1 - LOCATION OF REMAINING STRING                             Ÿ
                                    7733              Ÿ      R15 - CC=ZERO, ALL OK                                          Ÿ
                                    7734              Ÿ            CC=MINUS, NULL EXPRESSION                                Ÿ
                                    7735              Ÿ            CC=PLUS, ERROR, ERROR MSG TSEG'D.                        Ÿ
                                    7736              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ

                                    8428              Ÿ  EVLSTACK - EVALUATE EXPRESSION STACK                               Ÿ
                                    8429              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    8430              Ÿ  THIS ROUTINE SHOULD BE CALLED EACH TIME AN OPERATOR IS PLACED      Ÿ
                                    8431              Ÿ  ON THE EXPRESSION STACK.  RETURNED VALUE OF R1 MUST BE USED TO     Ÿ

                                   14031              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   14032              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   14033              Ÿ  XXXSCAN - SCAN EXPRESSION                                          Ÿ
                                   14034              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   14035              Ÿ  THIS ROUTINE SCANS THE NEXT ITEM IN THE EXPRESSION.                Ÿ
                                   14036              Ÿ  IF THE NEXT ITEM IS A OPERATOR OR A TERM, AN APPROPRIATE           Ÿ
                                   14037              Ÿ  EXPRESSION STACK ENTRY FOR THE ITEM IS GENERATED AND               Ÿ
                                   14038              Ÿ  PLACED AT THE EXPRESSION STACK.                                    Ÿ
                                   14039              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   14040              Ÿ  THIS ROUTINE RECURSIVELY CALLS XXXEVAL.                            Ÿ
                                   14041              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   14042              Ÿ  ON ENTRY:                                                          Ÿ
                                   14043              Ÿ       R0 - EXPRESSION STRING LENGTH                                 Ÿ
                                   14044              Ÿ       R1 - EXPRESSION STRING LOCATION                               Ÿ
                                   14045              Ÿ       R6 - EXPRESSION STACK POINTER                                 Ÿ
                                   14046              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   14047              Ÿ  ON EXIT:                                                           Ÿ
                                   14048              Ÿ       R0 - REMAINING STRING LENGTH                                  Ÿ
                                   14049              Ÿ       R1 - REMAINING STRING ADDRESS                                 Ÿ
                                   14050              Ÿ       R6 - EXPRESSION STACK ENTRY POINTER (NOT CHANGED)             Ÿ
                                   14051              Ÿ            EXPRESSION ENTRY MAY BE ONE OF THE FOLLOWING:            Ÿ
                                   14052              Ÿ               A) OPERATOR                                           Ÿ
                                   14053              Ÿ               B) VALUE OF TERM                                      Ÿ
                                   14054              Ÿ               C) END OF EXPRESSION                                  Ÿ
                                   14055              Ÿ      R15 - CC=ZERO, IF SCAN OK                                      Ÿ
                                   14056              Ÿ            CC=NZ, IF ERROR... ERROR MSG TSEG 'D                     Ÿ
                                   14057              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   14058              Ÿ       IF END OF EXPRESSION THEN R0=0 OR R1 POINTS TO ';'            Ÿ
                                   14059              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ

                                   15345              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   15346              Ÿ  THIS ROUTINE IS A WORK HORSE !!                                    Ÿ
                                   15347              Ÿ  IT HANDLES ALL NAMES IN EXPRESSIONS. CASES HANDLED ARE AS          Ÿ
                                   15348              Ÿ  FOLLOWS:                                                           Ÿ
                                   15349              Ÿ       1. WORD OPERATORS (LT, GT, ..)                                Ÿ
                                   15350              Ÿ       2. RESERVED WORDS                                             Ÿ
                                   15351              Ÿ       3. VARIABLES (LOCAL/GLOBAL/SYSTEM)                            Ÿ
                                   15352              Ÿ       4. SYSTEM VARIABLES                                           Ÿ
                                   15353              Ÿ       5. SYSTEM FUNCTIONS                                           Ÿ
                                   15354              Ÿ       6. ETC.. ETC..                                                Ÿ
                                   15355              Ÿ  EACH NAME IS EVALUATED, AND A VALUE IS PLACED ON THE               Ÿ
                                   15356              Ÿ  EXPRESSION STACK.  THIS ROUTINE ESSENTIALLY JUST FIGURES           Ÿ
                                   15357              Ÿ  OUT WHAT THE NAME IS (EG. VARIABLE, FUNCTION, ETC ,,,)             Ÿ
                                   15358              Ÿ  AND THEN CALLS A ROUTINE TO GET THE VALUE OF THE SPECIFIED         Ÿ

                                   15360              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ

                                   20050              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   20051              Ÿ  SCNOP - SCANNED AN OPEN PARENTHESIS "("                            Ÿ
                                   20052              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   20053              Ÿ  "(" INDICATES THE START OF A NEW EXPRESSION.  WE EVALUATE IT       Ÿ
                                   20054              Ÿ  BY RECURSIVELY CALLING XXXEVAL .                                   Ÿ
                                   20055              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   20056              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   20057              Ÿ  ON ENTRY:                                                          Ÿ
                                   20058              Ÿ       R1 - ADDRESS OF "(" IN EXPRESSION                             Ÿ
                                   20059              Ÿ       R0 - LENGTH OF EXPRESSION REMAINING                           Ÿ
                                   20060              Ÿ       R6 - EXPRESION STACK                                          Ÿ
                                   20061              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   20062              Ÿ  ON EXIT:                                                           Ÿ
                                   20063              Ÿ       R0 - LENGTH OF REMAINING EXPRESSION (UPDATED)                 Ÿ
                                   20064              Ÿ       R1 - ADDRESS OF REMAINING EXPRESSION (POINTS PAST ")")        Ÿ
                                   20065              Ÿ       R6 - VALUE OF PARENTHESIZED EXPRESSION PUT ON STACK           Ÿ
                                   20066              Ÿ      R15 - CC=ZERO, IF ALL OK                                       Ÿ
                                   20067              Ÿ            CC=NZ, IF ERROR... ERROR MSG TSEG 'D                     Ÿ
                                   20068              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   20069              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   20070              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ

                                   20761              Ÿ  WHENEVER WE HAVE JUST SCANNED A TERM (IE. VALUE).  IF NO           Ÿ
                                   20762              Ÿ  OPERATOR IS FOUND THEN WE RETURN, AN END OF EXPRESSION AND         Ÿ
                                   20763              Ÿ  RETURN R1,R0 AS THEY WERE ON ENTRY.                                Ÿ
                                   20764              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   20765              Ÿ  ON ENTRY:                                                          Ÿ
                                   20766              Ÿ       R0 - EXPRESSION STRING LENGTH                                 Ÿ
                                   20767              Ÿ       R1 - EXPRESSION STRING LOCATION                               Ÿ
                                   20768              Ÿ       R6 - EXPRESSION STACK POINTER                                 Ÿ
                                   20769              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   20770              Ÿ  ON EXIT:                                                           Ÿ
                                   20771              Ÿ       R0 - REMAINING STRING LENGTH                                  Ÿ
                                   20772              Ÿ       R1 - REMAINING STRING ADDRESS                                 Ÿ
                                   20773              Ÿ       R6 - EXPRESSION STACK ENTRY POINTER (NOT CHANGED)             Ÿ
                                   20774              Ÿ            EXPRESSION ENTRY MAY BE ONE OF THE FOLLOWING:            Ÿ
                                   20775              Ÿ               A) OPERATOR                                           Ÿ
                                   20776              Ÿ               B) END OF EXPRESSION                                  Ÿ
                                   20777              Ÿ      R15 - CC=ZERO, IF OPER FOUND, OR NOT FOUND                     Ÿ
                                   20778              Ÿ            CC=NZ, IF INVALID OPERATOR FOUND,, ERR MSG IS T'SEGD     Ÿ
                                   20779              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   20780              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ

0                                  28591              *
                                   28592              **
                                   28593              **  ZAP ROUTINES ---     for N0-N9
                                   28594              **
                                   28595              **  ZAP FOR OLD STYLE N0-N9.  THESE ZAPS ALLOW FOR INTEGER
                                   28596              **  VARIABLES IN EXPRESSIONS AND IN N0 THRU N9...  THESE
                                   28597              **  ZAPS ARE APPLIED ONLY IN OLD EXEC MODE.... SEE OLD EXEC
                                   28598              **  GUIDE FOR DETAILS...  HURRAH FOR BACKWARDS
                                   28599              **  COMPATABILITY !
                                   28600              **
                                   28601              **  ALL REQUIRED ZAPS ARE FOUND IN VARS, FUNC, AND EVAL MODULES !!
                                   28602              ** ----------------------------------------------------------------
                                   28603              **
                                   28604              **  RULES FOR INTEGER ZAPS:
                                   28605              **    1. MUST BE IN OLD EXEC MODE
                                   28606              **    2. N0-N9 ARE INTEGERS
                                   28607              **    3. LITTERALS ARE INTEGERS 2, 8, 12328, ETC.
                                   28608              **       (NUMBERS CONTAINING DECIMAL POINT ARE NOT !! EG 4.0 2. )
                                   28609              **    4. IF 2 INTEGERS ARE + - * OR /, THE RESULT IS AN INTEGER.
                                   28610              **    5. THE RESULT OF THE INT(..), NCONVERT(..), AND NHEX(..)
                                   28611              **       FUNCTIONS ARE INTEGERS.
                                   28612              **    6. IF NONE OF THE ABOVE RULES APPLY, THE NUMBER IS A NUMBER
                                   28613              **       AND NOT AN INTEGER.  (IE.  123.482 1.000 ETC)
                                   28614              **    7. SPECIFICALLY, ALL VARIABLES OTHER THAT N0-9 ARE NUMBERS.
                                   28615              **    8. AND, ALL FUNCTIONS OTHER THAN (RULE 4) RETURN NUMBERS.
                                   28616              **    9. NUMBERS MAY BE INTEGER VALUES, BUT ARE NOT CLOSED UNDER
                                   28617              **       DIVISION.
                                   28618              **   10. NOTE: IN NEW EXEC MODE ALL NUMBERS ARE NUMBERS AND !!
                                   28619              **             1/3 = 0.3333333
                                   28620              **   11. OH YEAH !
                                   28621              **
                                   28622              **  ZAPINTR6 - TURN ON INTEGER FLAG, VAR ENTRY @R6
